   1: // I-cd-022 (#612): pathname-aware AppShell gate. On `/`, suppress BOTH
   2: // the AppShell header AND its <main> wrapper so the home route can
   3: // provide its own header (with the same primary nav) + its own <main>.
   4: // This avoids G1 (double header) + G6 (nested main) landmark violations.
   5: //
   6: // Tiny "use client" boundary so the otherwise server-rendered AppShell
   7: // can still wrap every non-home route on the server.
   8: "use client";
   9: 
  10: import { usePathname } from "next/navigation";
  11: 
  12: import { AppShell } from "@/components/app_shell";
  13: 
  14: interface AppShellGateProps {
  15:   children: React.ReactNode;
  16: }
  17: 
  18: export function AppShellGate({ children }: AppShellGateProps) {
  19:   const pathname = usePathname();
  20:   // Home owns its own header + main; render children bare on `/`.
  21:   if (pathname === "/") {
  22:     return <>{children}</>;
  23:   }
  24:   return <AppShell>{children}</AppShell>;
  25: }

   1: /**
   2:  * POLARIS v6 API client.
   3:  *
   4:  * Mirrors the FastAPI contract in src/polaris_v6/api/{runs,health,stream}.py.
   5:  *
   6:  * I-carney-005 (2026-05-13): all requests are browser-relative paths so the
   7:  * browser only ever talks to the webui origin. Next.js server-side rewrites
   8:  * (web/next.config.ts) forward `/api/v6/*` → `${INTERNAL_API_URL}/*`, which
   9:  * in production compose is `http://api:8000` (a Docker service name the
  10:  * browser cannot resolve directly). In local dev, INTERNAL_API_URL defaults
  11:  * to http://localhost:8000 so `npm run dev` against a host-port-mapped
  12:  * backend works without any client-side configuration.
  13:  *
  14:  * Codex diff iter-1 P1-B: NEXT_PUBLIC_BACKEND_URL is no longer consulted at
  15:  * runtime — baking an absolute http://api:8000 into the client bundle would
  16:  * make production browsers attempt direct Docker-network reach and fail.
  17:  */
  18: 
  19: import { authHeader, redirectToSignIn } from "@/lib/auth";
  20: 
  21: const BACKEND_URL = "/api/v6";
  22: 
  23: /**
  24:  * I-rdy-004 (#500) — fetch wrapper for every v6 API call. Injects the
  25:  * `Authorization: Bearer <jwt>` header, preserves any caller-supplied
  26:  * headers, and does NOT force a content-type (so `FormData` uploads keep
  27:  * their auto-generated multipart boundary). On a 401 it clears the token
  28:  * and routes to /sign-in.
  29:  */
  30: async function authFetch(
  31:   url: string,
  32:   init: RequestInit = {},
  33: ): Promise<Response> {
  34:   const headers = new Headers(init.headers ?? {});
  35:   for (const [key, value] of Object.entries(authHeader())) {
  36:     headers.set(key, value);
  37:   }
  38:   const response = await globalThis.fetch(url, { ...init, headers });
  39:   if (response.status === 401) {
  40:     redirectToSignIn();
  41:   }
  42:   return response;
  43: }
  44: 
  45: /**
  46:  * I-rdy-004 — SSE URL for a run's event stream. Native `EventSource` cannot
  47:  * set request headers, so the JWT rides as the `access_token` query param;
  48:  * the backend `require_auth` accepts it for `/stream/*` paths only.
  49:  */
  50: export function streamUrl(runId: string): string {
  51:   const token = authHeader().Authorization?.replace(/^Bearer /, "");
  52:   const base = `${BACKEND_URL}/stream/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}`;
  53:   return token ? `${base}?access_token=${encodeURIComponent(token)}` : base;
  54: }

  68:   | "in_progress"
  69:   | "completed"
  70:   | "cancelled"
  71:   | "failed"
  72:   | "abort_scope_rejected"

  78:   template: TemplateId;
  79:   question: string;
  80:   document_ids?: string[];
  81: }

  83: export interface RunStatusResponse {
  84:   run_id: string;
  85:   status: RunStatus;
  86:   // I-rdy-011 (#507): true once a cancel has been requested; lets the run
  87:   // page show a cancel as in-flight before an in-progress run transitions.
  88:   cancel_requested?: boolean;
  89:   template: string;
  90:   question: string;
  91:   queued_at: string;
  92:   started_at?: string | null;
  93:   finished_at?: string | null;
  94: }
  95: 
  96: export interface ApiError extends Error {
  97:   status: number;
  98:   body: unknown;
  99: }
 100: 
 101: async function asJsonOrThrow<T>(response: Response): Promise<T> {
 102:   const body = await response.json().catch(() => null);
 103:   if (!response.ok) {
 104:     const error = new Error(
 105:       `POLARIS backend returned ${response.status}`,
 106:     ) as ApiError;
 107:     error.status = response.status;
 108:     error.body = body;
 109:     throw error;
 110:   }
 111:   return body as T;
 112: }
 113: 
 114: /**
 115:  * Thrown by createRun when POST /runs is rejected by the 1-concurrent-session
 116:  * constraint (I-rdy-013): a research run is already queued or in progress.
 117:  */
 118: export class ConcurrentRunError extends Error {
 119:   readonly activeRunId: string;
 120:   readonly activeStatus: string;
 121:   constructor(message: string, activeRunId: string, activeStatus: string) {
 122:     super(message);
 123:     this.name = "ConcurrentRunError";
 124:     this.activeRunId = activeRunId;
 125:     this.activeStatus = activeStatus;
 126:   }
 127: }
 128: 
 129: export async function createRun(
 130:   payload: RunRequest,
 131: ): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
 132:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs`, {
 133:     method: "POST",
 134:     headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
 135:     body: JSON.stringify(payload),
 136:   });
 137:   if (response.status === 409) {
 138:     // Read the body exactly once, then unwrap FastAPI's { detail: {...} }
 139:     // envelope. The 1-concurrent-session reject carries a structured detail;
 140:     // any other 409 falls through to a generic ApiError.
 141:     const body = (await response.json().catch(() => null)) as {
 142:       detail?: unknown;
 143:     } | null;
 144:     const detail = (body?.detail ?? body) as {
 145:       code?: string;
 146:       message?: string;
 147:       active_run_id?: string;
 148:       active_status?: string;
 149:     } | null;
 150:     if (detail && detail.code === "concurrent_run_active") {
 151:       throw new ConcurrentRunError(
 152:         detail.message ?? "A research run is already in progress.",
 153:         detail.active_run_id ?? "",
 154:         detail.active_status ?? "in_progress",
 155:       );
 156:     }
 157:     const error = new Error("POLARIS backend returned 409") as ApiError;
 158:     error.status = 409;
 159:     error.body = body;
 160:     throw error;
 161:   }
 162:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
 163: }
 164: 
 165: export async function getRun(runId: string): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
 166:   const response = await authFetch(`${BACKEND_URL}/runs/${runId}`);
 167:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
 168: }
 169: 
 170: // I-rdy-011 (#507): request cancellation of a run. A queued run cancels
 171: // instantly; an in-progress run aborts cooperatively at the next pipeline
 172: // stage boundary. Already-terminal runs are an idempotent no-op.
 173: export async function cancelRun(runId: string): Promise<RunStatusResponse> {
 174:   const response = await authFetch(
 175:     `${BACKEND_URL}/runs/${encodeURIComponent(runId)}/cancel`,
 176:     { method: "POST" },
 177:   );
 178:   return asJsonOrThrow<RunStatusResponse>(response);
 179: }

 191:   pass_rate: number;
 192:   retracted_source_ids?: string[] | null;
 193: }

 202: export async function fetchPin(

 204:   date: string,

// I-carney-005 P1-004 + P1-005: standalone output for Docker runner +
// server-side rewrite of /api/v6/* → ${INTERNAL_API_URL}/* so browser

// I-cd-015 (GH#611) — exclude test-harness routes from the production build.
//
// Listed routes (/charts_test/*, /sentence_hover_test/*,
// /disambiguation_modal_preview/*, /generation/*, /retrieval/*, /sse/*)
// are dev-only harness surfaces. In production deployments they must
// return 404 so reviewers + Carney's office don't reach internal test
// pages.
//
// Override: `POLARIS_TEST_HARNESS_ENABLED=1` keeps harness routes
// reachable (CI workflow `.github/workflows/web_ci.yml` runs
// `evidence_tooltip_perf.spec.ts` against `next start` in prod mode
// and needs `/sentence_hover_test/perf` to work). Real production
// deployment leaves this UNSET.
import { NextResponse } from "next/server";

export function middleware() {
  const isProd = process.env.NODE_ENV === "production";
  const harnessAllowed = process.env.POLARIS_TEST_HARNESS_ENABLED === "1";
  if (isProd && !harnessAllowed) {
    return new NextResponse(null, {
      status: 404,
      headers: { "x-harness-blocked": "1" },
    });
  }
  return NextResponse.next();
}

  38:     "/auth/login",
  39:     "/docs",       # FastAPI's own OpenAPI UI
  40:     "/redoc",
  41:     "/openapi.json",
  42: )
  43: 
  44: DEFAULT_ACCOUNTS_PATH = "/app/config/static_accounts.yaml"
  45: 
  46: _pwd_ctx = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")
  47: _bearer_scheme = HTTPBearer(auto_error=False)
  48: router = APIRouter(tags=["auth"])
  49: 
  50: 
  51: class LoginRequest(BaseModel):
  52:     username: str
  53:     password: str
  54: 
  55: 
  56: class LoginResponse(BaseModel):
  57:     access_token: str
  58:     token_type: str = "bearer"
  59:     role: str
  60:     expires_in: int  # seconds
  61: 
  62: 
  63: class User(BaseModel):
  64:     username: str
  65:     role: str

  67: 
  68: def _load_accounts() -> list[dict[str, Any]]:
  69:     """Read the static-accounts YAML. Raises RuntimeError if missing.
  70: 
  71:     LAW II: never silently default to an empty account list (which would
  72:     behave as 'allow nobody' but the operator would not realize the file
  73:     was missing).
  74:     """
  75:     path = Path(os.environ.get("POLARIS_STATIC_ACCOUNTS_PATH", DEFAULT_ACCOUNTS_PATH))
  76:     if not path.exists():
  77:         raise RuntimeError(
  78:             f"static_accounts.yaml not found at {path}. Set "
  79:             "POLARIS_STATIC_ACCOUNTS_PATH or mount the file. The application "
  80:             "refuses to start without the auth substrate (LAW II)."
  81:         )
  82:     body = yaml.safe_load(path.read_text(encoding="utf-8"))
  83:     if not isinstance(body, dict) or not isinstance(body.get("accounts"), list):
  84:         raise RuntimeError(f"static_accounts.yaml at {path} must have top-level 'accounts' list")
  85:     return body["accounts"]
  86: 
  87: 
  88: def _jwt_secret() -> str:
  89:     secret = os.environ.get("POLARIS_JWT_SECRET", "").strip()
  90:     if not secret or len(secret) < 32:
  91:         raise RuntimeError(
  92:             "POLARIS_JWT_SECRET env var missing or too short (<32 chars). "
  93:             "Application refuses to issue tokens with a weak/missing key (LAW II). "
  94:             "Set via AWS Secrets Manager → cloud-init → .env per I-carney-004."
  95:         )
  96:     return secret
  97: 
  98: 
  99: def verify_app_startup() -> None:
 100:     """Called at FastAPI app create_app() time. Fail loud if auth substrate
 101:     is misconfigured. Per LAW II, we never start an auth-gated app with a
 102:     broken auth gate.
 103: 
 104:     Skipped when POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED=1 (Phase-0 demo + tests).
 105:     """
 106:     if os.environ.get("POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED", "") == "1":
 107:         return
 108:     _jwt_secret()
 109:     _load_accounts()  # raises if YAML missing or malformed
 110: 
 111: 
 112: def issue_token(username: str, role: str) -> tuple[str, int]:
 113:     """Returns (jwt, expires_in_seconds)."""
 114:     expires_in = JWT_EXPIRY_HOURS * 3600
 115:     payload = {
 116:         "sub": username,
 117:         "role": role,
 118:         "iat": datetime.now(timezone.utc),
 119:         "exp": datetime.now(timezone.utc) + timedelta(hours=JWT_EXPIRY_HOURS),
 120:     }
 121:     token = jwt.encode(payload, _jwt_secret(), algorithm=JWT_ALGORITHM)
 122:     return token, expires_in
 123: 
 124: 
 125: def _path_is_public(path: str) -> bool:
 126:     return any(path.startswith(prefix) for prefix in PUBLIC_PATH_PREFIXES)
 127: 
 128: 
 129: async def require_auth(
 130:     request: Request,
 131:     creds: HTTPAuthorizationCredentials | None = Depends(_bearer_scheme),
 132: ) -> User | None:
 133:     """Global FastAPI dependency. None on public paths; raises 401 otherwise.
 134: 
 135:     Phase-0 demo: POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED=1 short-circuits to None (auth off).
 136:     """
 137:     if os.environ.get("POLARIS_AUTH_DISABLED", "") == "1":
 138:         return None
 139:     if _path_is_public(request.url.path):
 140:         return None
 141:     # Token resolution. Normal routes: Authorization: Bearer header. SSE
 142:     # (/stream/*): the browser's native EventSource cannot set request
 143:     # headers, so the JWT is accepted from the access_token query param —
 144:     # but ONLY for /stream paths, never for state-changing routes.
 145:     token: str | None = None
 146:     if creds is not None and creds.scheme.lower() == "bearer":
 147:         token = creds.credentials
 148:     elif request.url.path.startswith("/stream/"):
 149:         # Trailing slash: only the SSE route /stream/{run_id} — never a
 150:         # lookalike like /streaming/*.
 151:         token = request.query_params.get("access_token")
 152:     if not token:
 153:         raise HTTPException(
 154:             status_code=401,
 155:             detail={"error": "missing_bearer_token", "message": "Authorization: Bearer <jwt> required"},
 156:         )
 157:     try:
 158:         payload = jwt.decode(token, _jwt_secret(), algorithms=[JWT_ALGORITHM])
 159:     except JWTError as exc:
 160:         raise HTTPException(
 161:             status_code=401,
 162:             detail={"error": "invalid_token", "message": str(exc)},
 163:         ) from exc
 164:     return User(username=payload["sub"], role=payload.get("role", "reviewer"))
 165: 
 166: 
 167: @router.post("/auth/login", response_model=LoginResponse)
 168: def login(payload: LoginRequest) -> LoginResponse:
 169:     accounts = _load_accounts()
 170:     for account in accounts:
 171:         if account.get("username") == payload.username:
 172:             hashed = account.get("password_bcrypt", "")
 173:             if hashed and _pwd_ctx.verify(payload.password, hashed):
 174:                 token, exp_in = issue_token(payload.username, account.get("role", "reviewer"))
 175:                 return LoginResponse(
 176:                     access_token=token,
 177:                     role=account.get("role", "reviewer"),
 178:                     expires_in=exp_in,
 179:                 )
 180:             break
 181:     # Constant-time-ish failure shape (don't leak whether username exists).
 182:     raise HTTPException(
 183:         status_code=401,
 184:         detail={"error": "invalid_credentials"},
 185:     )
 186: 
 187: 
 188: def generate_strong_secret(n_bytes: int = 48) -> str:
 189:     """Helper for operator scripts: 64-char URL-safe random secret."""
 190:     return secrets.token_urlsafe(n_bytes)

 succeeded in 1035ms:
   1: /**
   2:  * I-rdy-004 (#500) — client-side auth: JWT store + login + header injection.
   3:  *
   4:  * Carney demo scope. The JWT is held in sessionStorage: survives a page
   5:  * refresh, cleared when the tab closes, not shared with a fresh tab —
   6:  * the safer browser-storage choice per the Codex I-rdy-004 brief review.
   7:  * 12h JWT expiry (matches the backend); cleared on any 401.
   8:  */
   9: 
  10: const TOKEN_KEY = "polaris_jwt";
  11: const EXPIRY_KEY = "polaris_jwt_expiry_ms";
  12: const DEFAULT_EXPIRY_SECONDS = 12 * 60 * 60;
  13: 
  14: export interface LoginResult {
  15:   ok: boolean;
  16:   status: number;
  17:   error?: string;
  18: }
  19: 
  20: function store(): Storage | null {
  21:   if (typeof window === "undefined") return null;
  22:   return window.sessionStorage;
  23: }
  24: 
  25: /** Current JWT, or null if absent or past its 12h expiry. */
  26: export function getToken(): string | null {
  27:   const s = store();
  28:   if (!s) return null;
  29:   const token = s.getItem(TOKEN_KEY);
  30:   const expiry = s.getItem(EXPIRY_KEY);
  31:   if (!token || !expiry) return null;
  32:   if (Date.now() >= Number(expiry)) {
  33:     clearToken();
  34:     return null;
  35:   }
  36:   return token;
  37: }
  38: 
  39: export function setToken(token: string, expiresInSeconds: number): void {
  40:   const s = store();
  41:   if (!s) return;
  42:   const ttl = expiresInSeconds > 0 ? expiresInSeconds : DEFAULT_EXPIRY_SECONDS;
  43:   s.setItem(TOKEN_KEY, token);
  44:   s.setItem(EXPIRY_KEY, String(Date.now() + ttl * 1000));
  45: }
  46: 
  47: export function clearToken(): void {
  48:   const s = store();
  49:   if (!s) return;
  50:   s.removeItem(TOKEN_KEY);
  51:   s.removeItem(EXPIRY_KEY);
  52: }
  53: 
  54: export function isAuthenticated(): boolean {
  55:   return getToken() !== null;
  56: }
  57: 
  58: /**
  59:  * POST credentials to the backend. On 200, store the JWT and report ok.
  60:  * A 401 here is invalid-credentials feedback for the sign-in form — it is
  61:  * NOT routed through the generic 401-redirect (that would loop the page).
  62:  */
  63: export async function login(
  64:   username: string,
  65:   password: string,
  66: ): Promise<LoginResult> {
  67:   let response: Response;
  68:   try {
  69:     response = await fetch("/api/v6/auth/login", {
  70:       method: "POST",
  71:       headers: { "content-type": "application/json" },
  72:       body: JSON.stringify({ username, password }),
  73:     });
  74:   } catch {
  75:     return {
  76:       ok: false,
  77:       status: 0,
  78:       error: "Could not reach POLARIS. Check the connection.",
  79:     };
  80:   }
  81:   if (response.status === 200) {
  82:     const body = (await response.json()) as {
  83:       access_token: string;
  84:       expires_in?: number;
  85:     };
  86:     setToken(body.access_token, body.expires_in ?? DEFAULT_EXPIRY_SECONDS);
  87:     return { ok: true, status: 200 };
  88:   }
  89:   if (response.status === 401) {
  90:     return { ok: false, status: 401, error: "Invalid username or password." };
  91:   }
  92:   return {
  93:     ok: false,
  94:     status: response.status,
  95:     error: `Sign-in failed (HTTP ${response.status}).`,
  96:   };
  97: }
  98: 
  99: /** Authorization header for the current token, or {} if unauthenticated. */
 100: export function authHeader(): Record<string, string> {
 101:   const token = getToken();
 102:   return token ? { Authorization: `Bearer ${token}` } : {};
 103: }
 104: 
 105: /** Clear the token and route to /sign-in. Called on a generic 401. */
 106: export function redirectToSignIn(): void {
 107:   if (typeof window === "undefined") return;
 108:   clearToken();
 109:   if (window.location.pathname !== "/sign-in") {
 110:     window.location.href = "/sign-in";
 111:   }
 112: }

  27:

  30:       .map(

  32:           `\n  - [${v.impact}] ${v.id}: ${v.description}\n    nodes: ${v.nodes

  41:       )

  43:     throw new Error(
  44:       `axe-core found ${results.violations.length} WCAG-AA violation(s):${summary}`,
  45:     );
  46:   }
  47: }

 159: test.describe("WCAG 2.5.8 target-size sweep (F-28 — broader than axe)", () => {
 160:   // axe's target-size rule has loose overlap-detection; cycle-8 P1.1 and
 161:   // P1.4 surfaced multiple <button>/<label>/<a role="button"> surfaces
 162:   // that pass axe but fail strict WCAG 2.2 SC 2.5.8 AA (24x24 minimum).
 163:   // This sweep walks every clickable element + asserts ≥24x24 directly.
 164: 
 165:   test("Dashboard — all clickable targets ≥24x24", async ({ page }) => {
 166:     await page.goto("/dashboard", { waitUntil: "networkidle" });
 167:     const small = await page.evaluate(() => {
 168:       const results: Array<{
 169:         tag: string;
 170:         text: string;
 171:         w: number;
 172:         h: number;
 173:       }> = [];
 174:       // Exclude <label htmlFor=...> — labels paired with a form control
 175:       // delegate the hit target to the control itself (WCAG 2.5.8 "inline"
 176:       // exemption). The "browse files" label has no htmlFor (it wraps the
 177:       // hidden file input directly) so it remains in scope.
 178:       const sel =
 179:         'button, label:not([for]), [role="button"], [role="radio"], a[href]';
 180:       document.querySelectorAll(sel).forEach((el) => {
 181:         if (!(el instanceof HTMLElement)) return;
 182:         const r = el.getBoundingClientRect();
 183:         if (r.width === 0 || r.height === 0) return; // hidden / pre-render
 184:         if (r.width < 24 || r.height < 24) {
 185:           results.push({
 186:             tag: el.tagName,
 187:             text: (el.textContent || "").trim().slice(0, 60),
 188:             w: Math.round(r.width),
 189:             h: Math.round(r.height),
 190:           });
 191:         }
 192:       });
 193:       return results;
 194:     });
 195:     if (small.length > 0) {
 196:       throw new Error(
 197:         `WCAG 2.5.8 failures (${small.length} target(s) < 24x24):\n` +
 198:           small
 199:             .map((s) => `  - ${s.tag} "${s.text}" → ${s.w}x${s.h}px`)
 200:             .join("\n"),
 201:       );
 202:     }
 203:   });

   1: "use client";
   2: 
   3: import { Suspense, useState } from "react";

   8: import { Button } from "@/components/ui/button";

  10:   Card,
  11:   CardContent,
  12:   CardDescription,
  13:   CardFooter,
  14:   CardHeader,
  15:   CardTitle,
  16: } from "@/components/ui/card";
  17: import { Input } from "@/components/ui/input";
  18: 
  19: /**
  20:  * I-cd-014 (GH#610): same-origin validation for `?next=` redirect.
  21:  *
  22:  * Rejects:
  23:  *   - non-string / empty values
  24:  *   - URL parse failures
  25:  *   - URLs that, when parsed against `window.location.origin`, resolve to
  26:  *     a different origin (protocol-relative `//evil.com`, absolute
  27:  *     `http://...`, backslash-as-separator `/\evil.com` — all caught by
  28:  *     the URL parser).
  29:  *   - fragment-only / hash-only navigation (e.g. `#frag`) — these are
  30:  *     same-origin but offer no real navigation, so we fall back to `/`.
  31:  *
  32:  * Returns the validated `pathname + search + hash` or `"/"`.
  33:  */
  34: function safeNextPath(next: string | null): string {
  35:   if (!next) return "/";
  36:   if (typeof window === "undefined") return "/";
  37:   try {
  38:     const parsed = new URL(next, window.location.origin);
  39:     if (parsed.origin !== window.location.origin) return "/";
  40:     // Reject fragment-only / hash-only / empty pathname — they leave the
  41:     // user on the sign-in route with just a fragment appended.
  42:     if (!parsed.pathname || parsed.pathname === "/sign-in") return "/";
  43:     return parsed.pathname + parsed.search + parsed.hash;
  44:   } catch {
  45:     return "/";
  46:   }
  47: }
  48: 
  49: /**
  50:  * I-cd-014 (GH#610): Next.js App Router requires `useSearchParams()` users
  51:  * to be wrapped in a Suspense boundary (or the route opts into dynamic
  52:  * rendering). Wrapping the form here is the lighter-weight choice and
  53:  * matches the existing repo convention.
  54:  */
  55: export default function SignInPage() {
  56:   return (
  57:     <Suspense fallback={<SignInPageFallback />}>
  58:       <SignInPageContent />
  59:     </Suspense>
  60:   );
  61: }
  62: 
  63: function SignInPageFallback() {
  64:   return (
  65:     <div className="bg-muted/40 flex min-h-screen flex-col items-center justify-center px-6 py-12">
  66:       <div
  67:         className="text-muted-foreground text-sm"
  68:         data-testid="sign-in-loading"
  69:       >
  70:         Loading sign-in…
  71:       </div>
  72:     </div>
  73:   );
  74: }
  75: 
  76: function SignInPageContent() {
  77:   const router = useRouter();
  78:   const searchParams = useSearchParams();
  79:   const [username, setUsername] = useState("");
  80:   const [password, setPassword] = useState("");
  81:   const [error, setError] = useState<string | null>(null);
  82:   const [pending, setPending] = useState(false);
  83: 
  84:   async function handleSubmit(e: React.FormEvent) {
  85:     e.preventDefault();
  86:     setError(null);
  87:     setPending(true);
  88:     const result = await login(username.trim(), password);
  89:     setPending(false);
  90:     if (result.ok) {
  91:       const next = safeNextPath(searchParams.get("next"));
  92:       router.push(next);
  93:       router.refresh();
  94:     } else {
  95:       setError(result.error ?? "Sign-in failed.");
  96:     }
  97:   }
  98: 
  99:   return (
 100:     <div className="bg-muted/40 flex min-h-screen flex-col items-center justify-center px-6 py-12">
 101:       <div className="flex w-full max-w-sm flex-col gap-6">
 102:         <div className="flex flex-col gap-1 text-center">
 103:           <span className="text-muted-foreground text-xs font-medium tracking-widest uppercase">
 104:             POLARIS Canada
 105:           </span>
 106:           <span className="text-foreground text-base font-semibold">
 107:             Sovereign Deep Research
 108:           </span>
 109:         </div>
 110: 
 111:         <Card>
 112:           <form onSubmit={handleSubmit} data-testid="sign-in-form">
 113:             <CardHeader>
 114:               <CardTitle>Sign in</CardTitle>
 115:               <CardDescription>
 116:                 Enter your POLARIS reviewer credentials.
 117:               </CardDescription>
 118:             </CardHeader>
 119:             <CardContent className="flex flex-col gap-4">
 120:               <div className="flex flex-col gap-2">
 121:                 <label
 122:                   htmlFor="username"
